# Text Elements
Core Exercize: ^rDyfJN7I

Each Chip Looks like This ^BeplQZbo

Name of Data field ^q69Tvuh6

28 ish bars, sum of bars width remains 
constant but number can change ^oYPuxfUN

(would be smarter like red -> green) ^BCRFJRPZ

Missing Data = Missing bar ^axoCXoPg

Arm Soreness: ^DS5FbNJZ

Lower Excercize: ^MkORR7Sk

Lower Soreness: ^46ehfcYv

Cardio: ^RqglsfID

Bleeding: ^eXT8im6W

Core Exercize: ^bURJIDB1

Core Soreness: ^3gOtfMJQ

Arm Excercize: ^hAvxkjIn

Sickness: ^iCv5jCav

Cramps: ^77DcbyVO

Analysis Page have chips stacked ^L7qHchc2

Chip order can be changed by dragging ^zikSplG2

Chips can be hidden ^p6nEAcDK

Bars on chips are time aligned, so you
 can see patterns / causations ^yhPvCL3M
